This delightful little salon is nestled in darling & quaint Brentwood. I travel here every 6 weeks from Livermore. The drive through the Altamont on Vasco Road is intoxicating; traversing the beautiful rolling hills, sprawling ranches, fruit stands and windmill farm.
Arriving in downtown Brentwood, it's like being transported back in time to "Mayberry". The town is pristine and untouched by commercialism.

Upon arriving inside Beauty Lounge, you are presented with warm colors, textures, and lighting, yet progressive styling stations. There is a very comfy and inviting waiting area in the entrance, as well. They carry all the best styling products.
It is apparent that the owners have a tremendous amount of pride and care into this lovely salon.
The folks here are are very professional and are always smiling and happy.

My coif consistently yields compliments. When people inquire who does my hair, I proudly recommend Beauty Lounge!!<//Text>

When a message is left on the voicemail, the call will always be returned as soon as possible.\nTo address your concern about the exam,  Dr Takher will always examine the condition of a tooth prior to making any treatment recommendations or giving any financial estimates.  Usually an xray is required for that, or at least a very recent xray from a previous dentist.  We do charge for this, but are happy to apply the charge to the cost of treatment when applicable.  We are simply unable to do quality work on teeth without the necessary diagnostic tools.\nThanks again, and we are happy you were able to find a dental office to take great care of you.'}</resp>< Text>

< Review>
I have been being treated by this Dental office for 20 years.  I was skeptical when the new Dentist Dr. Takher took over the practice, but I gave him a shot.  In the year or two, Dr. Takher and his team have been treating me my overall health has increased by 100%.  I have extreme anxiety and fear of having dental work performed and Dr. Takher and his team have alleviated that.  From Aubri at the front desk to Amber, Dr. Takher's assistant, the practice is stellar and friendly. I have to give special thanks and appreciation to Tyra, the best Dental Hygienist anywhere she has been cleaning my teeth for years and treated and cured me of minor gum disease that could have developed into a severe medical problem. <userid>109155575433485978194< /userid>< text>
Piano bar is... meh. Half dive bar, half music venue (I've never once heard a piano played). Some places are able to pull off a duel theme by bringing the best of both to the table. Unfortunately this place misses the mark. Of the few times I've been I found myself unimpressed and bored. One time a band was finishing and the next band wasn't going to perform for another hour and 45 minutes. That's just poor planning. I came to hear music, but now I've got to wait 1:45? I ended up leaving, I don't have that much time to be out.

Stick to beer and wine here, the craft drinks are as expected from a dive.

I've actually heard that this place is closing down soon. Not surprised.</text>

< text>
LIVE MUSIC!? Yes, please! There was some amazing musical talent at this bar!!! I really enjoyed watching the many different bands perform for everyone. The sound was really good, too - loud enough to enjoy but not too loud where you can't hear your friends talking to you.

Along with the music, the bar itself made me feel like I entered a different era.

We arrived before 10pm so it wasn't too crowded and getting drinks wasn't a struggle. By the time we left at around 11:45pm, there was a line outside, so I recommend getting there early!< /text>

<review>My husband and I discovered Mr. V's on our way to North Woods Inn.  On a whim, we had to give it a try (since our last name is V).  Without a reservation, the wait on a Friday night was an hour, but we were able to find a spot in the bar where we were able to get full service.  The live music was an amazing saxophonist.  The food was delicious and reasonably priced.  We enjoyed a couple Mediterranean dishes that were perfectly seasoned and prepared.  Our waitress, and all wait staff we encountered, we friendly, cordial and attentive to our needs. This place gets a 4 for the food and a 2 for bar service and a 5 for the service in the restaurant. It's right near work, so sometimes we'll splurge and go in on lunch, but that means we need to be quick. The waitress who services the bar is TERRIBLE. <user_name>Ryan Smith< /user_name>< Text>
So we came to Mr V's for the my parents in law wedding anniversary. The food was good. The frutti di marre was very good and the lamb shank was perfect. My ribeye was cooked perfectly but felt just a tad underseasoned but when paired with the peppercorn brandy sauce, the salt from the sauce elevated the steak. One thing we did notice which was inconsistent was the mac n cheese. One order tasted amazing and was freshly made and super cheesy, while the other felt like it was complemented with artificial cheese and tasted generic. The desserts were good though the tiramisu tasted unoriginal and needs elevation. The panna cotta was great and the creme brulee was delicious. The prices were reasonable for the food, and our waiter was fantastic. The bartender was also fantastic and our drinks were great.
In summary, if you're looking for a spot for a good steak and some good drinks go to Mr V's. There are some things to improve but overall the experience was a very good one<//Text>

< Review>
Excellent dining experience for all 16 people in our party. We chose Mr. V's for  our son and future-daughter-in-law's rehearsal dinner and it was a great choice. From the free valet parking to the time we finished the excellent desserts, everything was handled perfectly. The servers were outstanding as they got our drink orders right - - even when several people in our party had changed seats. The prices were very reasonable and the food was served quickly. (The prime rib was outstanding).

This was our second time going to Mr. V's. The first time was with our son who attends Biola University in La Mirada. The location is perfect as it is nearly walking distance from Biola or the surrounding dorm apartments.

Everyone had a great time and the service was exceptional. Very highly recommended and thanks to Mr. V's staff for such great food and service at an important event for our family.</Review>

<userid>108438697605497515191< /userid><Name>Chris Arellano<//Name>< Time>
1497076273107< /Time>
<Rating>2< /Rating>< review>
When we arrived they had complementary valet.  We were walk ins, and where promptly seated.

Our server Brent was great. Honest, attenitive, prompt  and polite.  Ordered drinks and shortly followed by complementary bread.

We started off with the a shirmp appetizer.  Which was a breaded shrimp serverd over broccoli.  Shrimp breading was soggy with a generic sauce, tasted like a frozen bag of premade shrimp and sauce, only doctored up with sesame seeds and steamed broccoli.  Sreving was too much, very unproportional for an appitizer!

Main course...

Ordered the rib eye, 16 oz (medium), rice pilaf, loaded bake potato.  Meat was cooked to ordered.  Meat was very chewy, like it was bought  from Stator Bros.  Lacked basic seasoning like SALT and pepper.  Bake potato was good and had a great presentation.  Rice was very bland, large chunks of veggies also seemed prepackaged.

Wife ordered prime rib,sauteed mushrooms.  Had good seasoning on the crust but did not transfer through out.  Very fatty cut.  Not marblized, just fatty.  Also way over cooked!

Dessert.

We orderd the lava cake and ice cream.  Came out in like 5 min!  Once again probably frozen and microwaved.  But wasnt bad, but had low expectations by that time.

Then went over to the bar area because they said they had live entertainment.  Was ramdom as can be.  Guy on a sax singing, TLC, Al Green...He was good but did not fit the ambiance

In conclusion, they are trying to be high end but food was sub par!  Like evey great steakhouse,  the food speaks for itself.  Either need to serve fresher, or made to order food.  Or get a better executive chef.  Seemed like a fast food Ruth Chris.

Only gets 2 stars do to excellent service!

Ps Brent you should apply for Ruth Chris, Mastro's, or 555.<//review>
